2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Deprecation Policy Enforcement

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that enforce the API deprecation policy: the deprecated API version warning injection, the removal version validation, and the minimum supported API version checks in the API server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

I am thinking...: Now I have a comprehensive picture of the files involved in API deprecation policy enforcement. Let me organize what I've found:

## Core API Deprecation Policy Enforcement Files

### 1. Deprecated API Version Warning Injection (apiserver)
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go` - Core logic: `IsDeprecated()`, `RemovedRelease()`, `WarningMessage()`, `MajorMinor()`
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go` - Injects deprecation warnings into API routes using the deprecation package
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go` - `AddWarningsHandler()` - wraps route handlers with warning injection
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go` - `AddWarning()`, `WithWarningRecorder()` - warning context management
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create.go` - Calls `WarningsOnCreate()` and adds warnings
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/update.go` - Calls `WarningsOnUpdate()` and adds warnings
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create_update.go` - Interface definitions for `WarningsOnCreate`/`WarningsOnUpdate`

### 2. CRD Deprecation Warning Injection

## Summary of Findings

The Kubernetes API deprecation policy enforcement spans several layers:

### 1. Core Deprecation Warning Injection (API Server)
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go`** — The heart of the system. Contains `IsDeprecated()`, `RemovedRelease()`, `WarningMessage()`, and `MajorMinor()` functions that check whether an API object is deprecated and construct warning messages.
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`** — Calls the deprecation functions during API route registration and wraps handlers with `AddWarningsHandler()` to inject `Warning` HTTP headers on every request to deprecated API versions.
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go`** — `AddWarningsHandler()` wraps route handlers to emit warnings.
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go`** — `AddWarning()` and `WithWarningRecorder()` for the warning context infrastructure.

### 2. Per-Object Warnings (WarningsOnCreate/WarningsOnUpdate)
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create_update.go`** — Interface definitions
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create.go`** and **`update.go`** — Call `WarningsOnCreate`/`WarningsOnUpdate` and emit warnings

### 3. CRD Deprecation
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`** — `defaultDeprecationWarning()` for CRD version deprecation

### 4. Removal Version Validation (prerelease-lifecycle-gen)
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/prerelease-lifecycle-gen/prerelease-lifecycle-generators/status.go`** — Code generator for `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and `APILifecycleRemoved()`
